Noto Dashboard

Noto Arimo

  • Development builds
  • Source repository
  • Report a bug in this font
Known Issues
  • Wrong weight value for Arimo-BoldItalic.ttf (#13)
  • [Arimo, Tinos, & Cousine] The Eng (U+014A) should be N-shaped (as opposed to n-) (#12)
  • Questionable glyph for U+1D24 LATIN LETTER VOICED LARYNGEAL SPIRANT (#11)
  • Several missing characters from croscore fonts (musical symbols, mathematical characters, small capital Q) (#10)
  • Latin: combining diacritics positioning broken on historical letters (#9)
  • Latin/IPA vertical bars design issues (#8)
  • in Arimo, ᵼᶥ should be based on ɩ (#2)
  • changes to U+1D7B U+1DA6 U+1DA7 in Arimo and Cousine (#7)
  • Latin upsilons design issues in Arimo and Cousine (#6)
  • jumping superscripts of different sizes and different optical weights in Arimo, Cousine and Tinos (#5)
  • combining cedilla is misplaced w.r.t. a lot of base characters in Arimo, Tinos, Cousine (#4)
  • ꞵ in Tinos which still needs serifs and ƛ should be λ with a stroke in Arimo and Cousine (#3)
  • Arimo metrics (#1)

  • Development builds

Known Issues

  • Cousine has spacing problems on Hebrew (#3)
  • Cousine doesn't support combining marks properly? (#1)

    •

    • 
				
  • Problem with subscripts in Noto Sans Javanese (#5)
    • 
				
  • Missing or wrong pasangan glyphs in Noto Sans Javanese (#4)
    • 
				
  • Problems on Pasangans on Noto Sans Javanese (2) (#3)
    • 
				
  • Problems on Pasangans on Noto Sans Javanese  (#2)
    • 
				
  • Javanese penyangga ꦀ U+A980 and cecakꦁ U+A981 appears on tarung ꦴ U+A9B4 instead of on the previous symbol.  Example: ꦀꦀ appears on o ꦎ symbol U+A98E when typing "om" [ꦎꦴꦀ] or if you type the penyangga first before tarung, it doesn't fuse [ ꦎꦀꦴ] (#1)

    •

  • Noto Sans Khmer UI variable font & phase III static font has minor string truncation problem (#4)

  • Baseline of Noto Sans Khmer UI variable font is not aligned with Latin script (#2)

Known Issues

			
    
				
  • Italic and/or oblique font style (#11)
    • 
				
  • Looped Thai won't build (#10)
    • 
				
  • Noto Sans Thai: U+F700 and U+F70F are missing (#9)
    • 
				
  • Missing substitution rule for uni0E2C loChula-thai (#7)
    • 
				
  • No contextual variants of U+0331 in Thai (#6)
    • 
				
  • Misplaced U+0331 COMBINING MACRON BELOW in Thai (#5)
    • 
				
  • Missing contextual form of U+0E0D THAI CHARACTER YO YING (#4)
    • 
				
  • U+0E4D THAI CHARACTER NIKHAHIT is reordered below tone marks (#3)
    • 
				
  • NotoSansThaiUI-ttf phase III font's stacked diacritics seems more compressed than the NotoSansThaiUI-VH.ttf's ones (#2)
    • 
				
  • some Thai character sequences go outside UI box for Noto Sans Thai UI and they shouldn't (#1)
    •
